Scilly</h1>\t\t\t<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">\n\t\t\t\t<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>\t\t\t\t<div id="contentSub"></div>\n\t\t\t\t<div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p>\n\nThe <b>list of shipwrecks of the Isles of Scilly</b> is a list of ships which sank on or near the <a href="/wiki/Isles_of_Scilly" title="Isles of Scilly">Isles of Scilly</a>.\n</p><p>The list includes ships that sustained a damaged hull, which were later  refloated and repaired.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Scilly-bartholomew02_large.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Scilly-bartholomew02_large.jpg/450px-Scilly-bartholomew02_large.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Scilly-bartholomew02_large.jpg/600px-Scilly-bartholomew02_large.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2017" data-file-height="1536" /></a>  <div class="toclevel-1 tocsection-101"><a href="#Further_reading"><span class="tocnumber">13</span> <span class="toctext">Further reading</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n</div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Before_1601">Before 1601</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Before 1601">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1305">1305</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 1305">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>an unnamed sailing vessel wrecked on Tresco. The <a href="/wiki/Coroner" title="Coroner">Coroner</a>, William le Poer, on the island to take charge of the salvaged cargo, was \xe2\x80\xb3seized by the mob\xe2\x80\xb3 led by Randulph de Blancminster, Lord of the Manor, and imprisoned until he was able to purchase his freedom.<sup id="cite_ref-Larn_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Larn-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1555">1555</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 1555">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>unidentified Spanish or Spanish\xe2\x80\x93Netherlands vessel on Bartholomew Ledge. The oldest wreck site in the Isles of Scilly protected under the <a href="/wiki/Protection_of_Wrecks_Act_1973" title="Protection of Wrecks Act 1973">Protection of Wrecks Act 1973</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Larn_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Larn-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1597">1597</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: 1597">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>February &#8212; the Spanish Fleet of Indies galleon <i><b>San Bartolom\xc3\xa9</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_Cross_of_Burgundy.svg/23px-Flag_of_Cross_of_Burgundy.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_Cross_of_Burgundy.svg/35px-Flag_of_Cross_of_Burgundy.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_Cross_of_Burgundy.svg/45px-Flag_of_Cross_of_Burgundy.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="500" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>)   was lost within the Isles of Scilly. She was carrying lead ingots and fragments of bronze bells.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> (Note: may refer to 1555 wreck above.)</li></ul>\n<h2><span id="1601.E2.80.931700"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1601\xe2\x80\x931700">1601\xe2\x80\x931700</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 1601\xe2\x80\x931700">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1616_or_1617">1616 or 1617</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 1616 or 1617">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>a ship (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/23px-Flag_of_England.svg.png" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/35px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/46px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="480" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>) equipped by <a href="/wiki/Sir_Walter_Raleigh" class="mw-redirect" title="Sir Walter Raleigh">Sir Walter Raleigh</a> at his own expense sank in a gale whilst outward bound to <a href="/wiki/Guyana" title="Guyana">Guiana</a> seeking gold.<sup id="cite_ref-Larn_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Larn-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1617">1617</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 1617">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>the <a href="/wiki/Full-rigged_pinnace" title="Full-rigged pinnace">pinnace</a> <i><b>Supply</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/23px-Flag_of_England.svg.png" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/35px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/46px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="480" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_England" title="Kingdom of England">Kingdom of England</a>) of the <a href="/wiki/East_India_Company" title="East India Company">East India Company</a> was driven aground on the Western Rocks whilst homeward bound from <a href="/wiki/Bantam_(city)" class="mw-redirect" title="Bantam (city)">Bantam</a> to London. Men and goods saved and she made a second voyage to <a href="/wiki/Java" title="Java">Java</a> in 1621 and reported as laid up, there, in 1623.<sup id="cite_ref-Larn_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Larn-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1636">1636</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 1636">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>24 March \xe2\x80\x93 sailing ship <i><b>Gift of God</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Flag_of_Scotland_%28traditional%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Scotland_%28traditional%29.svg.png" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Flag_of_Scotland_%28traditional%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Scotland_%28traditional%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Flag_of_Scotland_%28traditional%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_Scotland_%28traditional%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Scotland" title="Kingdom of Scotland">Kingdom of Scotland</a>) of <a href="/wiki/Kirkcaldy" title="Kirkcaldy">Kirkcaldy</a> was wrecked.<sup id="cite_ref-Larn_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Larn-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1641">1641</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 1641">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>23 September \xe2\x80\x93 the <a href="/wiki/Dartmouth,_Devon" title="Dartmouth, Devon">Dartmouth</a> based <i><b><a href="/wiki/Merchant_Royal_(English_ship)" class="mw-redirect" title="Merchant Royal (English ship)">Merchant Royal</a></b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/23px-Flag_of_England.svg.png" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/35px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/46px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="480" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_England" title="Kingdom of England">Kingdom of England</a>) foundered between <a href="/wiki/Land%27s_End" title="Land&#39;s End">Land\'s End</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cornwall" title="Cornwall">Cornwall</a> and the Isles of Scilly.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1645">1645</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 1645">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>July \xe2\x80\x93 the <a href="/wiki/Cavalier" title="Cavalier">Royalist</a> vessel <i><b>John</b></i> ran ashore after a skirmish with three <a href="/wiki/Roundhead" title="Roundhead">Parliamentary</a> ships.<sup id="cite_ref-Larn_1-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Larn-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> She was the flagship of the pirate <a href="/wiki/John_Mucknell" title="John Mucknell">John Mucknell</a>.</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1651">1651</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 1651">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>Two unidentified Royalist <a href="/wiki/Frigates" class="mw-redirect" title="Frigates">frigates</a> anchored under Hugh Hill (now the Garrison) and blockading St Mary\'s was driven ashore in a storm and thought to be total wrecks (not confirmed by research).<sup id="cite_ref-Larn_1-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Larn-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1665">1665</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 1665">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>18 January \xe2\x80\x94 while on her first voyage home from the <a href="/wiki/Maluku_Islands" title="Maluku Islands">Moluccas</a> and <a href="/wiki/Banten_(town)" title="Banten (town)">Bantam</a> to London, the East Indiaman ship <i><b><a href="/w/index.php?title=Royal_Oak_(cargo_ship)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Royal Oak (cargo ship) (page does not exist)">Royal Oak</a></b></i> (<a href="/wiki/File:British_East_India_Company_flag.svg" class="image"><img alt="British East India Company flag.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/British_East_India_Company_flag.svg/22px-British_East_India_Company_flag.svg.png" width="22" height="11" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/British_East_India_Company_flag.svg/33px-British_East_India_Company_flag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/British_East_India_Company_flag.svg/44px-British_East_India_Company_flag.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="720" data-file-height="360" /></a> <a href="/wiki/British_East_India_Company" class="mw-redirect" title="British East India Company">British East India Company</a>) was lost (probably) on Pednathise Head in the <a href="/wiki/Western_Rocks,_Isles_of_Scilly" title="Western Rocks, Isles of Scilly">Western Rocks</a>. Some of the crew managed to abandon ship and took to a \xe2\x80\xb3low rock\xe2\x80\xb3 where they were rescued fifty-two hours later. She was carrying <a href="/wiki/Black_pepper" title="Black pepper">peppercorns</a>, cloth and <a href="/wiki/Porcelain" title="Porcelain">porcelain</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Larn_1-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Larn-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Bayly_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bayly-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1667">1667</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 1667">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>22 December (first report) \xe2\x80\x94 three ships lost near Scilly.<sup id="cite_ref-Larn_1-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Larn-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>(first report) \xe2\x80\x94 unidentified vessel (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_Cross_of_Burgundy.svg/23px-Flag_of_Cross_of_Burgundy.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_Cross_of_Burgundy.svg/35px-Flag_of_Cross_of_Burgundy.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_Cross_of_Burgundy.svg/45px-Flag_of_Cross_of_Burgundy.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="500" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>) wrecked at an unknown location. A passenger complained that he was left on a rock for one or two days while the cargo was salvaged, saying "Valuing the goods more than my life".<sup id="cite_ref-Larn_1-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Larn-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1668">1668</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 1668">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>11 December \xe2\x80\x94 <a href="/wiki/Sixth-rate" title="Sixth-rate">sixth-rate</a> <i><b>Hind</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/English_Red_Ensign_1620.svg/23px-English_Red_Ensign_1620.svg.png" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/English_Red_Ensign_1620.svg/35px-English_Red_Ensign_1620.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/English_Red_Ensign_1620.svg/46px-English_Red_Ensign_1620.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1080" data-file-height="660" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a>) lost on Crim rocks.<sup id="cite_ref-Larn_1-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Larn-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1670">1670</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 1670">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>21 August (first report) \xe2\x80\x94 "A great ship has been lost about the Scillies, the afterpart of a wreck has been found."<sup id="cite_ref-Larn_1-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Larn-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1680">1680</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: 1680">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>11 January \xe2\x80\x94 <a href="/wiki/East_India_Company" title="East India Company">East India Company</a> ship <i><b>Phoenix</b></i> carrying <a href="/wiki/White_pepper#White_pepper" class="mw-redirect" title="White pepper">white pepper</a> and cloth wrecked on the Western Rocks. Much of the cargo was salvaged and sold on Scilly to <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Abney" title="Thomas Abney">Thomas Abney</a> who paid \xc2\xa3202 8s 1d for 269 pieces of Peerlongs.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1681">1681</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: 1681">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>December \xe2\x80\x94 A cargo vessel (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/23px-Flag_of_England.svg.png" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/35px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/46px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="480" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_England" title="Kingdom of England">Kingdom of England</a>) wrecked off St Agnes. The lighthouse keeper on St Agnes was found guilty of negligence for being inattentive to the light and for plundering some of the cargo.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1686">1686</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: 1686">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>February \xe2\x80\x94 <a href="/wiki/Dutch_East_India_Company" title="Dutch East India Company">Vereenigde Oostindische Compagnie</a> ship, <i><b>Prinses Maria</b></i> sank in shallow water near Silver Carn, north of Santaspery Neck within the Western Rocks. King <a href="/wiki/James_II_of_England" title="James II of England">James II</a> sent his yacht to salvage some of the cargo and in 1973 a diving team recovered <a href="/wiki/Spanish_colonial_real" title="Spanish colonial real">real coins</a>, iron cannon and timbers.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span id="1701.E2.80.931800"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1701\xe2\x80\x931800">1701\xe2\x80\x931800</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: 1701\xe2\x80\x931800">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="unknown_year">unknown year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: unknown year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>a French seventy\xe2\x80\x93four gun ship was wrecked on the Western Rocks whilst making an attempt to invade the islands, an accompanying frigate managed to evade the rocks and return to France.<sup id="cite_ref-Woodley_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Woodley-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1707">1707</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: 1707">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:HMS_Association_(1697).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/HMS_Association_%281697%29.jpg/220px-HMS_Association_%281697%29.jpg" width="220" height="148" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/HMS_Association_%281697%29.jpg/330px-HMS_Association_%281697%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/HMS_Association_%281697%29.jpg/440px-HMS_Association_%281697%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1252" data-file-height="840" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:HMS_Association_(1697).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The Scilly naval disaster of 1707</div></div></div>\n<ul><li>22 October \xe2\x80\x94 <b><a href="/wiki/HMS_Association" class="mw-redirect" title="HMS Association">HMS <i>Association</i></a></b>, <b><a href="/wiki/HMS_Eagle_(1679)" title="HMS Eagle (1679)">HMS <i>Eagle</i></a></b>, <b><a href="/wiki/HMS_Romney_(1694)" title="HMS Romney (1694)">HMS <i>Romney</i></a></b> and <b><a href="/wiki/HMS_Firebrand_(1694)" title="HMS Firebrand (1694)">HMS <i>Firebrand</i></a></b> (all <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain"><img alt="Kingdom of Great Britain" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg/23px-Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg.png" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg/35px-Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg/46px-Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1008" data-file-height="560" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a>) with the loss of nearly 2,000<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> souls; <b><a href="/wiki/HMS_Phoenix_(1694)" title="HMS Phoenix (1694)">HMS <i>Phoenix</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain"><img alt="Kingdom of Great Britain" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg/23px-Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg.png" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg/46px-Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1008" data-file-height="560" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a>) sustained a damaged hull but was later refloated and repaired (see <a href="/wiki/Scilly_naval_disaster_of_1707" title="Scilly naval disaster of 1707">Scilly naval disaster of 1707</a>).</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1720">1720</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: 1720">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>a Dutch ship lost on Great Wingletang Rock, St Agnes along with her cargo and crew.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-larnscilly_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larnscilly-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1727">1727</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: 1727">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li><i><b>William and Mary</b></i> from Jamaica<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1730">1730</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: 1730">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>a ship carrying wine from the <a href="/wiki/Canary_Islands" title="Canary Islands">Canary Islands</a> was wrecked on or near Rosevean. The master and a crewman were lashed to a rock for three days before rescue.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1733">1733</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: 1733">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>unknown ship carrying <a href="/wiki/Mahogany" title="Mahogany">mahogany</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Honduras" title="Gulf of Honduras">Bay of Honduras</a> to London went ashore on Melledgan. Only the captain and one crew managed to get away on a raft and drifted to Kitten Rock, north of Gugh where they were picked up days later.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1736">1736</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: 1736">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>9 October - <i><b>The Triumph</b></i> from Jamaica carrying 500 hogshead of sugar and a large quantity of rum.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1737">1737</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: 1737">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>a Dutch ship was wrecked in Wingletang Bay, St Agnes in a south-east gale. The master and one of the crew were lost.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1738">1738</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: 1738">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>November \xe2\x80\x94 the <i><b>Diana</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Naval_Flag_of_the_Kingdom_of_France_%28Civil_Ensign%29.svg/23px-Naval_Flag_of_the_Kingdom_of_France_%28Civil_Ensign%29.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Naval_Flag_of_the_Kingdom_of_France_%28Civil_Ensign%29.svg/35px-Naval_Flag_of_the_Kingdom_of_France_%28Civil_Ensign%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Naval_Flag_of_the_Kingdom_of_France_%28Civil_Ensign%29.svg/45px-Naval_Flag_of_the_Kingdom_of_France_%28Civil_Ensign%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="800" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_France" title="Kingdom of France">Kingdom of France</a>) of Calais wrecked on Mincarlo.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1739">1739</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: 1739">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>30 December \xe2\x80\x94 <i><b>Mermaid</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/23px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/35px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/46px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1008" data-file-height="560" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">Kingdom of Great Britain</a>) of Plymouth wrecked on Crow Bar.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1742">1742</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: 1742">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>9 March \xe2\x80\x94 <i><b>Nancy</b></i> carrying Bristol compound spirits, hemp, iron and gunpowder caught fire and blew up in New Grimsby. There was damage to several ships in the vicinity.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1743">1743</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: 1743">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>13 July \xe2\x80\x94 Dutch East India Company cargo ship <b><a href="/wiki/Hollandia_(1742_ship)" title="Hollandia (1742 ship)">VOC <i>Hollandia</i></a></b>, (<a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_Dutch_East_India_Company.svg" class="image"><img alt="Flag of the Dutch East India Company.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Flag_of_the_Dutch_East_India_Company.svg/22px-Flag_of_the_Dutch_East_India_Company.svg.png" width="22" height="15" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Flag_of_the_Dutch_East_India_Company.svg/33px-Flag_of_the_Dutch_East_India_Company.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Flag_of_the_Dutch_East_India_Company.svg/44px-Flag_of_the_Dutch_East_India_Company.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" /></a>) on her maiden voyage and bound from <a href="/wiki/Amsterdam" title="Amsterdam">Amsterdam</a> to <a href="/wiki/Jakarta" title="Jakarta">Batavia</a>, wrecked on the Gunner Rock, near <a href="/wiki/Annet,_Isles_of_Scilly" title="Annet, Isles of Scilly">Annet</a> with the loss of 276 souls.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> In 1971 Rex Cowan found the wreck, a large quantity of silver coins, along with bronze cannons and mortars.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Allsop_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Allsop-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1748">1748</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: 1748">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>27 February \xe2\x80\x94 <a href="/w/index.php?title=HMS_Lizard_(1744)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="HMS Lizard (1744) (page does not exist)">HMS&#160;<i>Lizard</i></a> (<span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain"><img alt="Kingdom of Great Britain" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg/23px-Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg.png" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg/35px-Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg/46px-Naval_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1008" data-file-height="560" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a>} wrecked on the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Stones_reef" class="mw-redirect" title="Seven Stones reef">Seven Stones reef</a> with the loss of one hundred lives in 1747.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Noall_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Noall-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1750">1750</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: 1750">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>unknown date \xe2\x80\x94 a large unidentified sailing vessel lost in the Gilstone area.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1752">1752</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: 1752">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>a Dutchman carrying cotton from <a href="/wiki/Smyrna" title="Smyrna">Smyrna</a> wrecked on Rosevean. There were no survivors.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1753">1753</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: 1753">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>20 May \xe2\x80\x94 the <i><b>Johanna</b></i> stranded at Little Smith, St Agnes; accounts differ as to year of loss and voyage details. Either registered at (or left) <a href="/wiki/Topsham,_Devon" title="Topsham, Devon">Topsham</a> for Swansea<sup id="cite_ref-Johanna_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Johanna-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> or from the Isle of Wight for Liverpool.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> or en route from South Shields to Liverpool.<sup id="cite_ref-Johanna_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Johanna-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1758">1758</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: 1758">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>30 December \xe2\x80\x94 the <i><b>Furnace</b></i> bound for <a href="/wiki/Gosport" title="Gosport">Gosport</a> with a cargo of brandy, oil, <a href="/wiki/Prune" title="Prune">prunes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rosin" title="Rosin">rosin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pewter" title="Pewter">pewter</a> wrecked on Broad Ledge near Guther\'s Island. Most of her cargo was saved by locals and Custom officers.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Cooper_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cooper-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1759">1759</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: 1759">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>January \xe2\x80\x94 while bound for Barcelona from London and Falmouth the <i><b>Vincento Farea</b></i> was lost at Scilly.<sup id="cite_ref-Todd_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Todd-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>23 February \xe2\x80\x94 schooner <i><b>Anna Adriana</b></i>  wrecked at Scilly with the loss of her crew and cargo.<sup id="cite_ref-Todd_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Todd-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1760">1760</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: 1760">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>a \xe2\x80\xb3Dutchman\xe2\x80\xb3 was lost on the rock Biggal of Melledgan. She was carrying wine and paper.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1762">1762</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: 1762">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>a French vessel was wrecked on Rosevean; six of the eighteen crew survived by clinging to floating timbers.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1764">1764</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: 1764">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>a Dutch galliot carrying wine and brandy from <a href="/wiki/Bordeaux" title="Bordeaux">Bordeaux</a> to <a href="/wiki/Hamburg" title="Hamburg">Hamburg</a> wrecked on the Lethegus Ledge, St Agnes. Accounts vary from no lives lost to three lives lost.<sup id="cite_ref-Cooper_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cooper-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>a vessel with coal for the beacon (St Agnes lighthouse) was wrecked on Burnt Island, St Agnes.<sup id="cite_ref-Noall_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Noall-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1767">1767</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: 1767">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>11 January  - <i><b>Seahorse</b></i> of Newcastle, John James, Master, bound from Cadiz to London, laden with currants, cream of tartar, Spanish wool and <a href="/wiki/Fustic" title="Fustic">fustick</a>, was wrecked near Old Grimsby<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1771">1771</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: 1771">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>an unidentified ship lost with all hands on Gugh (probably on the Cuckolds Ledge).<sup id="cite_ref-larnscilly_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larnscilly-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1773">1773</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: 1773">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>25 September \xe2\x80\x94 snow <i><b>Duke of Cumberland</b></i> from <a href="/wiki/Boston" title="Boston">Boston</a>, Massachusetts carrying oil, lumber, deal and other timber to London wrecked north-east of St Helen\'s.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1774">1774</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: 1774">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>1 February \xe2\x80\x94 <i><b> Royd</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/23px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/35px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/46px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1008" data-file-height="560" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">Kingdom of Great Britain</a>) of London was beached on rocks when she parted her cable. She was en route from Barcelona to Roscoff with brandy and wine.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1776">1776</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: 1776">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>A galliot was driven ashore while on a journey from Bordeaux to Hamburg with a cargo of coffee, sugar, indigo and wine, which was salvaged and put under lock and key. They were consequently stolen by a number of men. A Custom House boatman was sentenced to transportation for seven years and two women were acquitted.<sup id="cite_ref-vyvyan_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vyvyan-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1780">1780</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: 1780">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>31 August \xe2\x80\x94 brig <i><b>Tryal</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/23px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/35px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/46px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1008" data-file-height="560" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">Kingdom of Great Britain</a>) of Bristol wrecked in Crow Sound en route from <a href="/wiki/Saint_Kitts" title="Saint Kitts">St Christopher</a> with sugar.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>20 November \xe2\x80\x94 while carrying <a href="/wiki/Portland_stone" title="Portland stone">Portland stone</a> to Dublin, Weymouth brig <i><b>Charming Molly</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/23px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/35px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/46px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1008" data-file-height="560" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">Kingdom of Great Britain</a>) was stranded and lost on Bryher.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1781">1781</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: 1781">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>3 March \xe2\x80\x94 brig <i><b>Endeavour</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/23px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/35px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/46px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1008" data-file-height="560" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">Kingdom of Great Britain</a>) of Liverpool was beached and lost along with her cargo of herrings, coal, rum and brandy. She was bound for Portsmouth from her home port.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>an unidentified <a href="/wiki/Venice" title="Venice">Venetian</a> ship was wrecked on Crebawethan. She was out of <a href="/wiki/Marseilles" class="mw-redirect" title="Marseilles">Marseilles</a> carrying <a href="/wiki/Castile_soap" title="Castile soap">Castille soap</a>, wine <a href="/wiki/Almond" title="Almond">almonds</a> and oil for London. Eleven of her crew escaped the wreck by holding on to a mast which carried them to New Grimsby on Tresco.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1782">1782</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: 1782">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>2 February \xe2\x80\x94 a British cargo ship the <i><b>Lady Johanna</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/23px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/35px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/46px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1008" data-file-height="560" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">Kingdom of Great Britain</a>) wrecked at Little Smith, St Agnes. The cargo of cotton and rum was salvaged and taken to Plymouth whilst the wreck was sold and broken up.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Note: this is a different ship to the wreck on Little Smith in 1753.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>14 July \xe2\x80\x94 cargo ship the <i><b>Madonna de Carmine</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/Flag_of_Most_Serene_Republic_of_Venice.svg/23px-Flag_of_Most_Serene_Republic_of_Venice.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/Flag_of_Most_Serene_Republic_of_Venice.svg/35px-Flag_of_Most_Serene_Republic_of_Venice.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/Flag_of_Most_Serene_Republic_of_Venice.svg/46px-Flag_of_Most_Serene_Republic_of_Venice.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="300" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Venice" title="Republic of Venice">Republic of Venice</a>) hit the Golden Ball Bar, west of St Helen\'s. Bound from Rotterdam to Smyrna with cloth, the crew sold some of the cargo in order to pay for their passage to Falmouth. No lives lost. A <a href="/wiki/Scheduled_Ancient_Monument" class="mw-redirect" title="Scheduled Ancient Monument">Scheduled Ancient Monument</a> and also referred to as <i>Madonna de Carminic</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>an unidentified <a href="/wiki/Venice" title="Venice">Venetian</a> ship was wrecked on Crebawethan. She was out of <a href="/wiki/Marseilles" class="mw-redirect" title="Marseilles">Marseilles</a> carrying <a href="/wiki/Castile_soap" title="Castile soap">Castille soap</a>, wine <a href="/wiki/Almond" title="Almond">almonds</a> and oil for London. Eleven of her crew escaped the wreck by holding on to a mast which carried them to New Grimsby on Tresco.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1783">1783</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: 1783">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>24 January \xe2\x80\x94 brig <i><b>Oldenburger</b></i> carrying a general cargo from St Vincent to Ostend went ashore on Tresco in New Grimsby harbour.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>31 July \xe2\x80\x94 Agnetta wrecked.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>4 September \xe2\x80\x94 the <i><b>Financier</b></i> bound for London from <a href="/wiki/Charleston,_South_Carolina" title="Charleston, South Carolina">Charlestown</a>, <a href="/wiki/The_Carolinas" title="The Carolinas">Carolina</a> with tobacco, rice and <a href="/wiki/Indigo" title="Indigo">indigo</a> hit rocks near Annet and sank.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> In the same hour the <i><b>Nancy</b></i> (see 1784 for a different ship) carrying sugar and rum from Jamaica was wrecked near St Agnes with no loss of life. A third, unnamed, ship was also believed to have been lost with all hands.<sup id="cite_ref-Jones_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jones-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>25 November \xe2\x80\x94 while bound for Liverpool from Viborg with deals the <i><b>Sophia</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/23px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/35px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/46px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1008" data-file-height="560" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">Kingdom of Great Britain</a>) of London stranded and sank.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1784">1784</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: 1784">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>26 February \xe2\x80\x94 a New York transport vessel wrecked on the back of Bryher.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>26 February \xe2\x80\x94 the <a href="/wiki/Packet_ship" class="mw-redirect" title="Packet ship">packet ship</a> <i><b><a href="/wiki/Nancy_(1774_EIC_ship)" title="Nancy (1774 EIC ship)">Nancy</a></b></i>, carrying actress <a href="/wiki/Ann_Cargill" title="Ann Cargill">Ann Cargill</a> and her young child, struck the Gilstone in the Western Rocks and sank in deeper water near <a href="/wiki/Rosevear" class="mw-redirect" title="Rosevear">Rosevear</a> Ledges. Some of the crew and passengers took to a small boat which was dashed on Rosevear killing all aboard. In total 36 crew, 12 passengers, and 1 prisoner drowned.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-McFarland_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McFarland-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>31 December \xe2\x80\x94 the <i><b>Aurora</b></i> struck a sunken rock off Land\'s End and made it to the Isles of Scilly finally sinking in St Helen\'s Gap. Cargo salvaged and she was refloated.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1786">1786</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: 1786">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>24 December \xe2\x80\x94 brigantine <i><b>Duke of Cornwall</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/23px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/35px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/46px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1008" data-file-height="560" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">Kingdom of Great Britain</a>) of Penzance hit the Bartholomew Ledge and was beached on St Agnes. She was the <a href="/wiki/Duke_of_Cornwall#Dukes_of_Cornwall,_1337_creation" title="Duke of Cornwall">Duke of Cornwall\'s</a> private tin ship and was carrying a general cargo from London for Falmouth and Penzance, in the teeth of a violent gale. The crew were saved but little of her cargo was retrieved for the proprietors.<sup id="cite_ref-larnscilly_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larnscilly-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Duke_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Duke-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>24 December \xe2\x80\x94 brig  <i><b>Betsy</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/23px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/35px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/46px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1008" data-file-height="560" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">Kingdom of Great Britain</a>) from Chester, and heading for London, was lost between the Bartholomew Ledge and Perconger, St Agnes. She was carrying lead blocks and empty casks.<sup id="cite_ref-larnscilly_10-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larnscilly-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>24 December \xe2\x80\x94 <i><b>Dowson</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/23px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/35px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg/46px-Red_Ensign_of_Great_Britain_%281707-1800%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1008" data-file-height="560" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">Kingdom of Great Britain</a>) from Leverpool (Liverpool) lost on the Isles of Scilly in a gale.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>24 December \xe2\x80\x94 an unidentified sloop sank on the Isles of Scilly.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>24 December \xe2\x80\x94 an unidentified brig sank on the Isles of Scilly.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1788">1788</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: 1788">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>7 June \xe2\x80\x94 an unnamed <a href="/wiki/Virginian_(ship)" title="Virginian (ship)">Virginian</a> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281777-1795%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281777-1795%29.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281777-1795%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281777-1795%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281777-1795%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281777-1795%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="2470" data-file-height="1300" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>) lost in the Gilstone area of the Western Rocks.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1789">1789</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: 1789">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>5 June \xe2\x80\x94 brigantine <i><b>Eagle</b></i> of Charlestown carrying tobacco, rice and staves went ashore near St Agnes.<sup <b><a href="/wiki/HMS_Pegasus_(1779)" title="HMS Pegasus (1779)">HMS <i>Pegasus</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain"><img Hill, St Martin\'s.<sup id="cite_ref-Cooper_19-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cooper-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> She was originally seen with a broken mainmast, smashed decking and rigging trailing astern and encircled the islands three times before beaching herself.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span One sailor drowned.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span id="1801.E2.80.931900"></span><span class="mw-headline"
