Destroyed off the uninhabited island of Annet in a storm on December 14, 1907.</div></div></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1901">1901</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: 1901">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>22 June \xe2\x80\x94 four masted barque <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=SS_Falkland&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SS Falkland (page does not exist)"><i>Falkland</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_of_Great_Britain_and_Ireland" title="United Kingdom of Great Britain and Ireland">United Kingdom</a>) of Liverpool struck the Crebinacks and drifted onto the Bishop\'s Rock where she foundered with several of the crew drowning. Two passengers and twenty-one of the crew made it on to the ship\'s boat which was piloted to St Mary\'s by the St Agnes lifeboat.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-McFarland3_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McFarland3-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1902">1902</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: 1902">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>2 February \xe2\x80\x94 sailing ship <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=SS_Lofaro&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SS Lofaro (page does not exist)"><i>Lofaro</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Italy_%281861%E2%80%931946%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861%E2%80%931946%29.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Italy_%281861%E2%80%931946%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861%E2%80%931946%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Italy_%281861%E2%80%931946%29.svg/45px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861%E2%80%931946%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1000" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Italy" title="Kingdom of Italy">Kingdom of Italy</a>) sunk off St Martin\'s Head with the loss of the crew despite attempts by the gig <i>Emperor</i> to save them. The <i>Lofaro</i> figurehead is currently in the <a href="/wiki/Tresco_Abbey_Gardens#Valhalla_collection" title="Tresco Abbey Gardens">Valhalla Museum</a> on Tresco.<sup id="cite_ref-Cooper_19-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cooper-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-McFarland3_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McFarland3-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1903">1903</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: 1903">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>17 June \xe2\x80\x94 <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_upon_Tyne" title="Newcastle upon Tyne">Newcastle</a> steamer <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=SS_James_Spier&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SS James Spier (page does not exist)"><i>James Spier</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_of_Great_Britain_and_Ireland" title="United Kingdom of Great Britain and Ireland">United Kingdom</a>)  bound for <a href="/wiki/Bastia" title="Bastia">Bastia</a> from Liverpool was rammed in dense fog by Norwegian barque <i><b>Magdelen</b></i> 30 miles SSW. She lost her mizzen mast and was towed to Penzance by steam trawler <i>Buckhound</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-Carter_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Carter-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>20 September \xe2\x80\x94 barque <i><b>Queen Mab</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_of_Great_Britain_and_Ireland" title="United Kingdom of Great Britain and Ireland">United Kingdom</a>) of Glasgow was 105 days out of <a href="/wiki/Punta_Arenas" title="Punta Arenas">Punta Arenas</a> when she struck the Spanish Ledges. She was bound for Falmouth, with <a href="/wiki/Maclura_tinctoria" title="Maclura tinctoria">fustic log-wood</a> and had passed the Wolf Rock on the 18th but was forced back by a strong, easterly gale. She was holed as she sailed over the Spanish Ledges and was then piloted by the St Agnes gig <i>O &amp; M</i> to anchorage off the southern tip of Samson. Found to be taking in water, and under tow by the island\'s packet steamer <i><a href="/wiki/West_Cornwall_Steam_Ship_Company#Lyonesse" title="West Cornwall Steam Ship Company">Lyonesse</a></i>, she was escorted to harbour with the assistance of the St Mary\'s and the St Agnes (<i>James and Caroline</i>) lifeboats. Thirteen local men manned the pumps for over five hours, and she made it to Hugh Town where she grounded at the harbour entrance. She was salvaged and left, on tow, for Falmouth and Le Havre on 7 October.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-larnscilly_10-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larnscilly-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-McFarland3_39-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McFarland3-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>17 October \xe2\x80\x94 while entering Crow Sound on a journey from Glasgow to Nova Scotia with a general cargo, the <i><b>Kilkeel</b></i> hit the Hats. She was later refloated.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1904">1904</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: 1904">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>13 August \xe2\x80\x94 <a href="/wiki/HMS_Decoy_(1894)" title="HMS Decoy (1894)"><i><b>HMS Decoy</b></i></a> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="720" data-file-height="360" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a>) a <a href="/wiki/Daring_class_destroyer_(1893)" class="mw-redirect" title="Daring class destroyer (1893)"><i>Daring</i> class</a> torpedo boat destroyer in collision with <a href="/wiki/HMS_Arun_(1903)" title="HMS Arun (1903)">HMS&#160;<i>Arun</i></a> off the <a href="/wiki/Isles_of_Scilly" title="Isles of Scilly">Isles of Scilly</a> with the loss of one life.</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1906">1906</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: 1906">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>3 June \xe2\x80\x94 steam-trawler <i><b>Magdalene</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>) of <a href="/wiki/Boulogne-sur-Mer" title="Boulogne-sur-Mer">Boulogne</a>, despite passing on the wrong side of the buoy while entering St Mary\'s Roads to seek medical assistance for an injured member of crew, managed to miss the Bartholmew Ledges. When leaving for sea the following day she again took the wrong route and this time struck the Ledges and sank two hours later.<sup id="cite_ref-larnscilly_10-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larnscilly-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>5 June \xe2\x80\x94 steam-trawler <i><b>General Roberts</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_of_Great_Britain_and_Ireland" title="United Kingdom of Great Britain and Ireland">United Kingdom</a>) of <a href="/wiki/Kingston_upon_Hull" title="Kingston upon Hull">Hull</a> sank after taking on water in the fishing grounds north of St Martin. Her crew abandoned ship in the punt and rowed towards Round Island.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>22 July \xe2\x80\x94 2126 ton King Line steamer <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=SS_King_Cadwallon&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SS King Cadwallon (page does not exist)"><i>King Cadwallon</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_of_Great_Britain_and_Ireland" title="United Kingdom of Great Britain and Ireland">United Kingdom</a>) bound for Naples with a cargo of coal from Barry, was lost on the Hard Lewis rocks to the east of St Martin\'s.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Allsop_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Allsop-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-McFarland3_39-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McFarland3-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>21 August \xe2\x80\x94 steam-trawler <i><b>Grassholm</b></i> damaged her bows on Great Minalto while trying to make anchorage during thick fog. She was on passage to Cardiff with fish. St Mary\'s Lifeboat <i>Henry Dundas</i> towed her to harbour.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1907">1907</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: 1907">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>14 December \xe2\x80\x94 <i><b><a href="/wiki/Thomas_W._Lawson_(ship)" title="Thomas W. Lawson (ship)">Thomas W. Lawson</a></b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281896-1908%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281896-1908%29.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281896-1908%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281896-1908%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281896-1908%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281896-1908%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="539" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>), the world\'s only seven-masted schooner going as bulk oil carrier in charter for the Anglo-American Oil Co. Bound for London from Philadelphia the huge schooner was caught in a northwest gale off the <a href="/wiki/Isles_of_Scilly" title="Isles of Scilly">Isles of Scilly</a> on 13 December 1907.  The captain and engineer were found the following day on South Carn in the Hellweather Rocks by a gig\'s crew which included the son of the pilot who was out searching for his father.<sup id="cite_ref-McFarland3_39-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McFarland3-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Mothersole_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mothersole-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1909">1909</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: 1909">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>14 August \xe2\x80\x94 the <i><b>Plympton</b></i> struck the Lethegus\' Ledge off St Agnes in thick fog. All the crew were saved but a man and boy from Hugh Town were lost when the boat went down without warning as they were unloading the cargo of grain which she was carrying from Villa Constitution to Dublin via Falmouth.<sup id="cite_ref-Allsop_16-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Allsop-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Mothersole_42-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mothersole-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1910">1910</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: 1910">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>18 April \xe2\x80\x94 <b><a href="/wiki/SS_Minnehaha" title="SS Minnehaha">SS <i>Minnehaha</i></a></b>, first-class liner hit Scilly Rock off Bryher in dense fog. Later refloated with no loss of life.<sup id="cite_ref-McFarland3_39-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McFarland3-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1911">1911</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: 1911">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>8 January \xe2\x80\x94 <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=SS_Ardencraig&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SS Ardencraig (page does not exist)"><i>Ardencraig</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_of_Great_Britain_and_Ireland" title="United Kingdom of Great Britain and Ireland">United Kingdom</a>) off the Gunners, abandoned by the crew and foundered about three o\'clock in the afternoon in the North West Channel.<sup id="cite_ref-McFarland3_39-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McFarland3-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>13 January \xe2\x80\x94 <i><b>Georges</b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Auray" title="Auray">Auray</a> was found, by the St Mary\'s lifeboat <i>Henry Dundas</i> on the 12th, at anchor near St Agnes with a light burning but no one on board. Out from Swansea for Trinite with 170 tons of coal she lost her sails in a gale and started to leak. Her crew abandoned and landed safely on St Agnes and she sank the next morning.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>26 March \xe2\x80\x94 steamship <i><b>Setiembre</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7d/Flag_of_Spain_%281785%E2%80%931873%2C_1875%E2%80%931931%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Spain_%281785%E2%80%931873%2C_1875%E2%80%931931%29.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7d/Flag_of_Spain_%281785%E2%80%931873%2C_1875%E2%80%931931%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Spain_%281785%E2%80%931873%2C_1875%E2%80%931931%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7d/Flag_of_Spain_%281785%E2%80%931873%2C_1875%E2%80%931931%29.svg/45px-Flag_of_Spain_%281785%E2%80%931873%2C_1875%E2%80%931931%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="500" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>) struck The Hats in Crow Sound and sank. She was a total loss despite her crew dumping her cargo of iron-ore overboard in an attempt to refloat her. Her boiler can still be seen above low water.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1912">1912</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: 1912">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>8 December \xe2\x80\x94 steamer <i><b>Antonios</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Greece.svg/23px-Flag_of_Greece.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Greece.svg/35px-Flag_of_Greece.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Greece.svg/45px-Flag_of_Greece.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="400" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a>) lost on Old Bess with the loss of her crew. The wreck went unnoticed for three days until wreckage and thousands of oranges were washed up on St Agnes.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1913">1913</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: 1913">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>14 August \xe2\x80\x94 the <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=SS_Susanna&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SS Susanna (page does not exist)"><i>Susanna</i></a></b>, on <a href="/wiki/Zantman%27s_Rock" title="Zantman&#39;s Rock">Zantman\'s Rock</a></li>\n<li>November \xe2\x80\x94 the <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=SS_Thornlichank&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SS Thornlichank (page does not exist)"><i>Thornlichank</i></a></b>, 2,105 tons of the Bank Line Limited, on a voyage from Iquique to London, wrecked on Crim Rock.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1914">1914</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: 1914">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>23 June \xe2\x80\x94 <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=SS_Gothland&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SS Gothland (page does not exist)"><i>Gothland</i></a></b> struck the Crim with a \xe2\x80\xb3consignment of Belgium undesirables\xe2\x80\xb3 deported from the USA. The passengers were landed on St Mary\'s and later taken to Cornwall on the <a href="/wiki/SS_Lyonesse_(1889)" title="SS Lyonesse (1889)"><i>Lyonesse</i></a>. The <i>Gothland</i> was refloated.<sup id="cite_ref-McFarland3_39-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McFarland3-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="World_War_I">World War I</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=72" title="Edit section: World War I">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1915">1915</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=73" title="Edit section: 1915">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>1 May \xe2\x80\x94 <a href="/wiki/Neutrality_(philosophy)" title="Neutrality (philosophy)">neutral</a> tanker <i><b><a href="/wiki/Gulflight" title="Gulflight">Gulflight</a></b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1900" data-file-height="1000" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>) torpedoed by <a href="/wiki/SM_U-30_(Germany)" title="SM U-30 (Germany)"><i>U-30</i></a>, commander: Erich von Rosenberg-Gruszczynski (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281903-1918%29.svg/23px-War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281903-1918%29.svg.png" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281903-1918%29.svg/35px-War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281903-1918%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281903-1918%29.svg/46px-War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281903-1918%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="360" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Imperial_German_Navy" title="Imperial German Navy">Imperial German Navy</a>) and later refloated.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1916">1916</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=74" title="Edit section: 1916">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>18 May \xe2\x80\x94 armed auxiliary <a href="/wiki/Naval_trawler" title="Naval trawler">naval trawler</a> <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=HMT_Carbineer&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="HMT Carbineer (page does not exist)">HMT&#160;<i>Carbineer</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="720" data-file-height="360" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a>) struck one of the <a href="/wiki/Crim_Rocks" title="Crim Rocks">Crim Rocks</a> and was run ashore at <a href="/wiki/Western_Rocks,_Isles_of_Scilly#Great_Crebawethan" title="Western Rocks, Isles of Scilly">Great Crebawethan</a> becoming a total loss.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>November \xe2\x80\x94 <a href="/wiki/Admiralty" title="Admiralty">Admiralty</a> <a href="/wiki/Auxiliary_ship" title="Auxiliary ship">auxiliary supply ship</a> <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=SS_Brodfield&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SS Brodfield (page does not exist)"><i>Brodfield</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Government_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Government_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Government_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Government_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Government_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Government_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_of_Great_Britain_and_Ireland" title="United Kingdom of Great Britain and Ireland">United Kingdom</a>) went ashore at the Giant\'s Castle, St Mary\'s whilst in ballast from <a href="/wiki/Le_Havre" title="Le Havre">Le Havre</a> to South Wales. Several attempts to refloat her were unsuccessful.<sup id="cite_ref-McFarland3_39-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McFarland3-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1917">1917</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=75" title="Edit section: 1917">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>11 May \xe2\x80\x94 two ships were wrecked on the same day during heavy fog, the SS <i><b>Italia</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Civil_Ensign_of_Italy.svg/23px-Civil_Ensign_of_Italy.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Civil_Ensign_of_Italy.svg/35px-Civil_Ensign_of_Italy.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Civil_Ensign_of_Italy.svg/45px-Civil_Ensign_of_Italy.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1000" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a>), a steam collier was wrecked on the Great Wingletang Rock off St Agnes, and the SS <i><b>Lady Charlotte</b></i>, another <a href="/wiki/Collier_(ship_type)" class="mw-redirect" title="Collier (ship type)">collier</a>, was lost, shortly before, at Porth Hellick on St Mary\'s. The <i>Italia</i> was carrying coal from Cardiff to <a href="/wiki/Taranto" title="Taranto">Taranto</a> and went aground at 15:30 and quickly sank. The only witness, a St Agnes girl was not believed and the wreckage that washed up was believed to belong to the <i>Lady Charlotte</i>. When the crew of the <i>Italia</i> reached St Mary\'s it was assumed that she had been torpedoed somewhere off the islands, as none of the crew could speak English. The Wingletang wreck was finally identified in 1964 when her serial number was found on the ship\'s patent log.<sup id="cite_ref-larnscilly_10-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larnscilly-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>5 October \xe2\x80\x94 schooner <i><b>Annie F. Conlon</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1900" data-file-height="1000" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>) was badly damaged by gunfire from a German submarine, and was towed to Crow Sound, where she began to break up. Her cargo of 455 casks of oil made \xc2\xa31,406 9s for her owners Marine Transport of Mobile, <a href="/wiki/Alabama" title="Alabama">Alabama</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>6 December \xe2\x80\x94 <b><a href="/wiki/USS_Jacob_Jones_(DD-61)" title="USS Jacob Jones (DD-61)">USS <i>Jacob Jones</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1900" data-file-height="1000" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a>), American destroyer was hit in the stern by a torpedo while on convoy duty. She exploded killing her crew and sank within eight minutes 25 miles SE of the Bishop Rock.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1918">1918</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=76" title="Edit section: 1918">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>10 November \xe2\x80\x94 Admiralty tug <i><b>Blazer</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Government_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Government_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Government_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Government_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Government_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Government_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_of_Great_Britain_and_Ireland" title="United Kingdom of Great Britain and Ireland">United Kingdom</a>) struck the Garrison. All her crew of 24 survived.<sup id="cite_ref-McFarland3_39-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McFarland3-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span id="1918.E2.80.931939"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1918\xe2\x80\x931939">1918\xe2\x80\x931939</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=77" title="Edit section: 1918\xe2\x80\x931939">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1920">1920</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=78" title="Edit section: 1920">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>2 December \xe2\x80\x94 SS <i><b>Hathor</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Merchant_flag_of_Germany_%281919%E2%80%931933%29.svg/23px-Merchant_flag_of_Germany_%281919%E2%80%931933%29.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Merchant_flag_of_Germany_%281919%E2%80%931933%29.svg/35px-Merchant_flag_of_Germany_%281919%E2%80%931933%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Merchant_flag_of_Germany_%281919%E2%80%931933%29.svg/45px-Merchant_flag_of_Germany_%281919%E2%80%931933%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Weimar_Republic" title="Weimar Republic">Germany</a>) wrecked on the Lethurges to the south of St Agnes. After breaking down near the <a href="/wiki/Azores" title="Azores">Azores</a> she was taken under tow by two German tugs who abandoned her in a gale off Scilly after the tow broke. Her crew was saved by lifeboat <i>Elsie</i> (<a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg" class="image"><img alt="Flag of the Royal National Lifeboat Institution.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/25px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png" width="25" height="17" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/38px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/50px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="500" /></a> <a href="/wiki/Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution" title="Royal National Lifeboat Institution">Royal National Lifeboat Institution</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-McFarland3_39-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McFarland3-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> She lies on the wreck of the <i>Plympton</i> which sank on 14 August 1909.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Allsop_16-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Allsop-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1921">1921</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=79" title="Edit section: 1921">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>20 January \xe2\x80\x94 <a href="/wiki/HMS_K5" title="HMS K5">HMS <i><b>K5</b></i></a>, (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="720" data-file-height="360" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a>) British submarine, about 120&#160;mi (190&#160;km) south-west of the Isles of Scilly with the loss of fifty-seven lives.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>11 July \xe2\x80\x94 SS <i><b>The Western Front</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1900" data-file-height="1000" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>) foundered several miles west of the Isles of Scilly when she caught fire after an explosion. She was carrying 7,000 tons of naval stores, including <a href="/wiki/Naphtha" title="Naphtha">naphtha</a>, <a href="/wiki/Turpentine" title="Turpentine">turpentine</a> and <a href="/wiki/Resin" title="Resin">resin</a> from <a href="/wiki/Jacksonville" class="mw-redirect" title="Jacksonville">Jacksonville</a> to London. One member of crew lost his life.<sup id="cite_ref-McFarland3_39-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McFarland3-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1925">1925</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=80" title="Edit section: 1925">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>21 March \xe2\x80\x94 steam-trawler <i><b>Cit\xc3\xa9 de Verdun</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>) struck Rosevear in a snowstorm. The crew of thirty landed, lit a fire and sent distress signals which were answered by the St Mary\'s lifeboat, <i>Elsie</i> (<a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg" class="image"><img alt="Flag of the Royal National Lifeboat Institution.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/25px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png" width="25" height="17" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/38px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/50px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="500" /></a> <a href="/wiki/Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution" title="Royal National Lifeboat Institution">Royal National Lifeboat Institution</a>). The nameboards of the trawler can still be seen in the Mermaid and Atlantic public houses on St Mary\'s.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>12 June \xe2\x80\x94 steam-trawler <i><b>Europe</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>) of <a href="/wiki/Boulogne" class="mw-redirect" title="Boulogne">Boulogne</a> struck Rosevear in fog. As the tide rose the trawler floated off the rocks and made for <a href="/wiki/Dunkirk" title="Dunkirk">Dunkirk</a> with slight damage.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1927">1927</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=81" title="Edit section: 1927">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>27 October \xe2\x80\x94 SS <i><b>Isabo</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Civil_Ensign_of_Italy.svg/23px-Civil_Ensign_of_Italy.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Civil_Ensign_of_Italy.svg/35px-Civil_Ensign_of_Italy.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Civil_Ensign_of_Italy.svg/45px-Civil_Ensign_of_Italy.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1000" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a>) with a cargo of grain foundered on Scilly Rock, west of Bryher. Three small boats <i>Czar</i>, <i>Ivy</i> and <i>Sunbeam</i> saved thirty-one men. Conditions deteriorated by the time lifeboat <i>Elsie</i> (<a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg" class="image"><img alt="Flag of the Royal National Lifeboat Institution.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/25px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png" width="25" height="17" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/38px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/50px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="500" /></a> <a href="/wiki/Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution" title="Royal National Lifeboat Institution">Royal National Lifeboat Institution</a>) arrived and she had to leave four men clinging to the rigging, returning the next day to pick them up along with one on the Scilly Rock. (The account of the rescue differs with twenty-eight or thirty-six men saved out of a crew of thirty-eight).<sup id="cite_ref-Wreck_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Wreck-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>26 December \xe2\x80\x94 sailing barge <i><b>Daphne</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>) of <a href="/wiki/Rochester,_Kent" title="Rochester, Kent">Rochester</a> was abandoned by her crew and foundered one mile east of St Mary\'s with her main sail lost. With her jib set she sailed on into Crow Sound and grounded on Tresco. Three days later she was towed to St Mary\'s as <a href="/wiki/Marine_salvage" title="Marine salvage">salvage</a>, repaired and returned to Rochester.<sup id="cite_ref-McFarland3_39-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McFarland3-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1938">1938</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=82" title="Edit section: 1938">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>12 September \xe2\x80\x94 <i><b>Pasteur</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>), a fishing vessel from <a href="/wiki/Camaret-sur-Mer" title="Camaret-sur-Mer">Camaret</a> stranded on Hanjaque. She was a regular visitor to Scillonian and Cornish waters fishing for crayfish.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> She was refloated on the next high tide.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="World_War_II">World War II</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=83" title="Edit section: World War II">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1939">1939</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=84" title="Edit section: 1939">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>22 December 1939 \xe2\x80\x94 the Clyde Shipping Company\'s ship <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=SS_Longships&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SS Longships (page does not exist)"><i>Longships</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>) was wrecked on the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Stones_reef" class="mw-redirect" title="Seven Stones reef">Seven Stones</a> reef near the spot where the <a href="/wiki/SS_Torrey_Canyon" title="SS Torrey Canyon"><i>Torrey Canyon</i></a> was later lost. The 27 crew was rescued by the St Mary\'s Lifeboat (<a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg" class="image"><img alt="Flag of the Royal National Lifeboat Institution.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/25px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png" width="25" height="17" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/38px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/50px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="500" /></a> <a href="/wiki/Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution" title="Royal National Lifeboat Institution">Royal National Lifeboat Institution</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-Noall_17-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Noall-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1944">1944</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=85" title="Edit section: 1944">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>20 June 1944 \xe2\x80\x94 <b><a href="/wiki/HMS_Warwick_(D25)" title="HMS Warwick (D25)">HMS <i>Warwick</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="720" data-file-height="360" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a>) sunk off the islands by <i><a href="/wiki/German_submarine_U-413" title="German submarine U-413">U-413</a></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg/23px-War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg.png" width="23" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kriegsmarine" title="Kriegsmarine">Kriegsmarine</a>), German <a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boat</a><sup id="cite_ref-Innes_McCartney_2002_51-0" U-1209">U-1209</a></b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg/23px-War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg.png" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" class="mw-headline" id="1945">1945</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=86" title="Edit section: 1945">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>12 January 1945 \xe2\x80\x94 merchant ship torpedoed off Scilly.<sup id="cite_ref-Bowden_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bowden-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>21 January 1945 \xe2\x80\x94 <i><b><a href="/wiki/German_submarine_U-1199" title="German submarine U-1199">U-1199</a></b></i> (<span />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kriegsmarine" title="Kriegsmarine">Kriegsmarine</a>), German U-boat.<sup id="cite_ref-Innes_McCartney_2002_51-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Innes_McCartney_2002-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>24 February 1945 \xe2\x80\x94 <i><b>Oriskany</b></i>, fruit cargo ship.</li>\n<li>24 February 1945 \xe2\x80\x94 <i><b><a src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg/23px-War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg.png" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg/35px-War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg/46px-War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kriegsmarine" title="Kriegsmarine">Kriegsmarine</a>), German U-boat.<sup id="cite_ref-Innes_McCartney_2002_51-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Innes_McCartney_2002-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>11 March 1945 \xe2\x80\x94 <i><b><a href="/wiki/German_submarine_U-681" title="German submarine U-681">U-681</a></b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg/23px-War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg.png" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg/35px-War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg/46px-War_Ensign_of_Germany_%281938-1945%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kriegsmarine" title="Kriegsmarine">Kriegsmarine</a>), hit either the Bishop Rock or the Crebinicks. She was badly damaged, tried to make for a neutral port in Ireland but was attacked by an American <a href="/wiki/Consolidated_B-24_Liberator" title="Consolidated B-24 Liberator">Liberator plane</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> The crew scuttled her off <a href="/wiki/Norrard_Rocks#Mincarlo" title="Norrard Rocks">Mincarlo</a><sup id="cite_ref-Bowden_50-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bowden-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Innes_McCartney_2002_51-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Innes_McCartney_2002-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> or 4 miles (6.4&#160;km) to the north-east of the Isles of Scilly.<sup id="cite_ref-U681_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-U681-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span id="1946.E2.80.932000"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1946\xe2\x80\x932000">1946\xe2\x80\x932000</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=87" title="Edit section: 1946\xe2\x80\x932000">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1949">1949</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=88" title="Edit section: 1949">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>6 October \xe2\x80\x94 the 6,300 ton <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=SS_Fantree&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SS Fantree (page does not exist)"><i>Fantree</i></a></b> (or <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=SS_Fantee&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SS Fantee (page does not exist)"><i>Fantee</i></a></b>) (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>) of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Dempster_Line" class="mw-redirect" title="Elder Dempster Line">Elder Dempster Line</a>, en route from West Africa to Liverpool via Amsterdam and carrying a cargo of hardwood, palm kernels, palm oil, cocoa, rubber, cotton, coffee beans and <a href="/wiki/Copal" title="Copal">copal</a> struck the Seven Stones reef in dense fog. The 53 crew and passengers managed to launch the ship\'s two lifeboats and many of the mahogany logs were salvaged by local boatman.<sup id="cite_ref-Noall_17-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Noall-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Liddiard_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Liddiard-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1951">1951</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=89" title="Edit section: 1951">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>10 September \xe2\x80\x94 the Isles of Scilly packet steamer SS <i><b><a href="/wiki/Scillonian_(1925)" title="Scillonian (1925)">Scillonian</a></b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Civil_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>) ran ashore on the Wingletang Rock in fog. She was later refloated and continued in service.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> The 54 passengers were taken to Hugh Town by the company launch <i>Kittern</i> which went ashore on Rat Island damaging her rudder before finally making it to harbour.<sup id="cite_ref-larnscilly_10-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larnscilly-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1955">1955</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=90" title="Edit section: 1955">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>21 January \xe2\x80\x94 <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=SS_Mando&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SS Mando (page does not exist)"><i>Mando</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Flag_of_Panama.svg/23px-Flag_of_Panama.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Flag_of_Panama.svg/35px-Flag_of_Panama.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Flag_of_Panama.svg/45px-Flag_of_Panama.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="450" data-file-height="300" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Panama" title="Panama">Panama</a>) a former <a href="/wiki/Liberty_ship" title="Liberty ship">liberty ship</a>, previously known as <i>Stepas Darius</i>,  drifted onto Golden Ball bar 0.5 miles west of St Helens when her engines failed. She was en route from <a href="/wiki/Hampton_Roads" title="Hampton Roads">Hampton Roads</a> to Rotterdam with 9,000 tons of coal. The captain was initially reluctant to leave his ship and twenty-five crew were saved by the St Mary\'s lifeboat <i>Cunard</i>. A <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Monuments_and_Archaeological_Areas_Act_1979" title="Ancient Monuments and Archaeological Areas Act 1979">Scheduled Ancient Monument</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>22 July 1955 \xe2\x80\x94 Panamanian registered steamer <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=SS_Punta&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SS Punta (page does not exist)"><i>Punta</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Flag_of_Panama.svg/23px-Flag_of_Panama.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Flag_of_Panama.svg/35px-Flag_of_Panama.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Flag_of_Panama.svg/45px-Flag_of_Panama.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="450" data-file-height="300" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Panama" title="Panama">Panama</a>) drove onto the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Stones_reef" class="mw-redirect" title="Seven Stones reef">Seven Stones reef</a> and was abandoned by her crew. She filled and sank soon afterwards.</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1961">1961</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=91" title="Edit section: 1961">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>9 March \xe2\x80\x94 trawler <i><b>Petit Jean Yves</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>) went aground near Cuckolds Carn, Gugh. She was refloated the next day with the help of the <a href="/wiki/St_Mary%27s_Lifeboat_Station" title="St Mary&#39;s Lifeboat Station">St Mary\'s lifeboat</a> (<a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg" class="image"><img alt="Flag of the Royal National Lifeboat Institution.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/25px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png" width="25" height="17" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/38px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg/50px-Flag_of_the_Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="500" /></a> <a href="/wiki/Royal_National_Lifeboat_Institution" title="Royal National Lifeboat Institution">Royal National Lifeboat Institution</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-larnscilly_10-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larnscilly-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1970">1970</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=92" title="Edit section: 1970">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>25 February \xe2\x80\x94 channel trawler <i><b>Jean Gougy</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>) was lost on the <a href="/wiki/Western_Rocks,_Isles_of_Scilly" title="Western Rocks, Isles of Scilly">Western Rocks</a>. The exact location is unknown, but wreckage and a body were washed up on Tresco. The other thirteen crew were never found.</li>\n<li>15 April \xe2\x80\x94 the MV <i><b>Poleire</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Cyprus.svg/23px-Flag_of_Cyprus.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Cyprus.svg/35px-Flag_of_Cyprus.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Cyprus.svg/45px-Flag_of_Cyprus.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Cyprus" title="Cyprus">Cyprus</a>) transporting zinc ore to Poland was wrecked on the Little Kettle Rock north of Tresco, and rapidly sank.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1976">1976</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=93" title="Edit section: 1976">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>29 September \xe2\x80\x94 the <a href="/wiki/Fish_factory_ship" class="mw-redirect" title="Fish factory ship">fish factory ship</a> <i><b>Rarau</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Romania.svg/23px-Flag_of_Romania.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Romania.svg/35px-Flag_of_Romania.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Romania.svg/45px-Flag_of_Romania.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="400" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romania</a>) was wrecked on the Seven Stones, where she later sank, although the crew were all rescued.<sup id="cite_ref-Liddiard_55-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Liddiard-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1977">1977</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=94" title="Edit section: 1977">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>13 February \xe2\x80\x94 <a href="/wiki/St_Malo" class="mw-redirect" title="St Malo">St Malo</a> trawler <i><b>Enfant du Bretagne</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>) was lost on Pednathise, within the <a href="/wiki/Western_Rocks,_Isles_of_Scilly#Other_named_rocks_and_reefs" title="Western Rocks, Isles of Scilly">Western Rocks</a> at night. The lifeboat came within hearing distance of the crew, but all drowned in the heavy seas before they could be brought aboard.<sup id="cite_ref-larn92_5-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larn92-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1979">1979</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=95" title="Edit section: 1979">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>August \xe2\x80\x94 <a href="/wiki/1979_Fastnet_race" title="1979 Fastnet race">Fastnet race</a>, many racing yachts sank in extreme weather</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1997">1997</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=96" title="Edit section: 1997">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:MV_Cita_wrecked_on_the_Isles_of_Scilly.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/MV_Cita_wrecked_on_the_Isles_of_Scilly.jpg/220px-MV_Cita_wrecked_on_the_Isles_of_Scilly.jpg" width="220" height="148" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/MV_Cita_wrecked_on_the_Isles_of_Scilly.jpg/330px-MV_Cita_wrecked_on_the_Isles_of_Scilly.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/MV_Cita_wrecked_on_the_Isles_of_Scilly.jpg/440px-MV_Cita_wrecked_on_the_Isles_of_Scilly.jpg 2x" data-file-width="444" data-file-height="298" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:MV_Cita_wrecked_on_the_Isles_of_Scilly.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>MV Cita</div></div></div>\n<ul><li>26 March \xe2\x80\x94 <b><a href="/wiki/MV_Cita" title="MV Cita">MV&#160;<i>Cita</i></a></b> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Flag_of_Antigua_and_Barbuda.svg/23px-Flag_of_Antigua_and_Barbuda.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Flag_of_Antigua_and_Barbuda.svg/35px-Flag_of_Antigua_and_Barbuda.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Flag_of_Antigua_and_Barbuda.svg/45px-Flag_of_Antigua_and_Barbuda.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="690" data-file-height="460" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Antigua_and_Barbuda" title="Antigua and Barbuda">Antigua and Barbuda</a>), German-owned cargo ship wrecked at Newfoundland Point, St Mary\'s. She was en route to Ireland and on automatic pilot whilst the crew slept. The St Mary\'s lifeboat took all nine Polish crew ashore.<sup id="cite_ref-Allsop_16-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Allsop-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Since_2001">Since 2001</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=97" title="Edit section: Since 2001">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2005">2005</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_shipwrecks_of_the_Isles_of_Scilly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=98" title="Edit section: 2005">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>4 July \xe2\x80\x94 trawler <i><b>Sauveterre</b></i> (<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" title="France">France</a>) sank sixty miles off the Isles of Scilly<sup id="cite_ref-Wreck_48-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Wreck-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span
